# HD/4K Integrated Camera — Interface Specifications

## Compatible model Table

**Mar. 1, 2025 — Panasonic Entertainment & Communication Co. Ltd.**

> Markdown transcription of the official PDF
> [InterfaceSpecifications_CompatibleModelTable_E.pdf](https://eww.pass.panasonic.co.jp/pro-av/support/content/guide/DEF/InterfaceSpecifications_CompatibleModelTable_E.pdf)
> (49 pages). The *Camera command* table (pages 2–31) and the *PT command* table
> (pages 32–37), each spread over many pages in the PDF, are merged into **one**
> continuous table here. The [※ Details](#-details) section covers pages 38–49.

### Legend

| Symbol | Meaning |
|---|---|
| ○ | Command is supported by the model |
| --- | Command is not supported by the model |
| ※ | See the [※ Details](#-details) section |
| `supports only …` | The model supports only the stated subset of the values |

Line breaks inside a cell are rendered as `<br>`. Values stacked in the `Data` and
`Data Contents` columns line up position by position, as in the original.
The PDF uses two visually identical characters for "supported" (U+25CB `○` and
U+3007 `〇`); both are normalised to `○` here. The original spelling, including its
typos (e.g. "Response to contol"), is kept as-is.
